${{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = spatial background metric
${{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = difference of spatial metric and spatial background metric
${{{ \gamma} _i} _j} = {{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} + {{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j}}$ = spatial metric

${{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial background metric derivative
${{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = difference of spatial metric derivative and spatial background metric derivative, hyperbolic state variable
${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial metric derivative
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$

${{{ b} ^i} _j} = {{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}}$
${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}} = {{{ b} ^i} _j}$

connections:
${{{{ \Gamma} _i} _j} _k} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\left({{{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k} _{,j}}} - {{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,i}}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \Gamma} _i} _k} _j} + {{{{ \Gamma} _j} _k} _i}}$

${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{\frac{1}{2}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,m}}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _k} _{,j}}}\right)}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _m} _j} - {{{{ \hat{d}} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _m} _j} - {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _m} _j} _k}}}\right)}}}$

metric inverse partial:
${{\left( {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}\right)} _{,k}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _m} _{,k}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _m} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _m}}\right)}}}}$

$\alpha$ = lapse

log lapse derivative:
${{ a} _i} = {{\left( \log\left( \alpha\right)\right)} _{,i}}$
${{ a} _i} = {{\frac{1}{\alpha}} {{ \alpha} _{,i}}}$
${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}}}$

Bona-Masso lapse evolution:
${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{{{ \alpha} _{,i}}} {{{ \beta} ^i}}} - {{{{\alpha}^{2}}} {{f}} {{\left({{{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}} - {{{2}} {{\Theta}}}}\right)}}}}$
${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}}$

lapse parameter
${{ f} _{,k}} = {{{f'}} \cdot {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}}}$

hyperbolic alpha var time evolution
${{{ \alpha} _{,t}} _{,k}} = {{{{4}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}} + {{{2}} {{f}} {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{{ f} _{,k}}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{{ a} _i} _{,k}}}} - {{{{ f} _{,k}}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}}} - {{{f}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}}} - {{{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}}}}$
using ${{ f} _{,k}} = {{{f'}} \cdot {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}}}$
${{{ \alpha} _{,t}} _{,k}} = {{{{4}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}} + {{{2}} {{f}} {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{f'}} \cdot {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{{ a} _i} _{,k}}}} - {{{f'}} \cdot {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}}} - {{{f}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}}} - {{{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}}}}$
using ${{{ \alpha} _{,t}} _{,k}} = {{ { \alpha} _{,k}} _{,t}}$ ; ${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}}}$
${{{{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{ a} _k}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{f'}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}} + {{{4}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ a} _k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{{ a} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}} {{{ a} _k}}} + {{{{{{ a} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^i} _{,k}}}} - {{{f'}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{\frac{1}{\alpha}}{\left({{{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{f'}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{\alpha}^{3}}}} + {{{4}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ a} _k}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{{ a} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}} {{{ a} _k}}} + {{{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^i} _{,k}}}} - {{{f'}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{\alpha}^{3}}}}} - {{{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}}} + {{{{{{2}} {{f}} {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}} - {{{f}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}}} - {{{2}} {{f}} {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}}} - {{{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{ a} _k}}}}}\right)}}$
using ${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{f'}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ a} _k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{{ a} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{{ a} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^i} _{,k}}}} - {{{f'}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _m} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _m}}\right)}}}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{f'}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ a} _k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{{ a} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ a} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^i} _{,k}}}} - {{{f'}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}}} + {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _m}}} + {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _m}}} + {{{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}$
using ${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}} = {{{ b} ^i} _j}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{f'}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ a} _k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{{ a} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ a} _i}} {{{{ b} ^i} _k}}} - {{{f'}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{\alpha}^{2}}}}} + {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _m}}} + {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _m}}} + {{{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}$

metric evolution:
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{{{-2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}} + {{{ \beta} _i} _{,j}} + {{{ \beta} _j} _{,i}}} - {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} _k} _i} _j}}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{{-2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,j}}} {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _k} _{,j}}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,i}}} {{{{ \gamma} _j} _k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,i}}}} + {{{-2}} {{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} _k} _i} _j}}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,j}}} {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _k} _{,j}}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,i}}} {{{{ \gamma} _j} _k}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,i}}}} - {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} _k} _i} _j}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \Gamma} _i} _j} _k} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\left({{{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k} _{,j}}} - {{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,i}}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,j}}} {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _k} _{,j}}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,i}}} {{{{ \gamma} _j} _k}}} + {{{{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,i}}}} - {{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _k} _i} _{,j}}}}} - {{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _k} _j} _{,i}}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}}$
symmetrizing ${{ \gamma} _i} _j$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,j}}} {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,i}}} {{{{ \gamma} _j} _k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}}$
using ${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}} = {{{ b} ^i} _j}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^k} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k}}} + {{{{{ b} ^k} _i}} {{{{ \gamma} _j} _k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^k} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k}}} + {{{{{ b} ^k} _i}} {{{{ \gamma} _j} _k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}}\right)}}}}$

metric delta evolution
${{\left( {{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} + {{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j}\right)} _{,t}} = {{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^k} _j}} {{\left({{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _k} + {{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _k}}\right)}}} + {{{{{ b} ^k} _i}} {{\left({{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _k} + {{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _k}}\right)}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{\left({{{ {{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}}\right)}}}}$
${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _k}} {{{{ b} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _k}} {{{{ b} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _k}} {{{{ b} ^k} _i}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _k}} {{{{ b} ^k} _i}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}} - {{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,t}}}}$
using ${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$ ; ${{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _k}} {{{{ b} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _k}} {{{{ b} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _k}} {{{{ b} ^k} _i}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _k}} {{{{ b} ^k} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}}} + {{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}} - {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}}}}$

metric partial delta evolution:
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,t}} _{,k}} = {{{-{{{2}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ \beta} ^l} _{,k}}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ \beta} ^l} _{,k}}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} - {{{2}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$ ; ${{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{-{{{2}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _j} _l}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _j} _l}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ \beta} ^l} _{,k}}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ \beta} ^l} _{,k}}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} - {{{2}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}}}\right)}}$
using ${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}}}$ ; ${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}} = {{{ b} ^i} _j}$

symmetrizing indexes
${{{ Z} _k} _{,t}} = {{{{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{ Z} _k} _{,l}}}} + {{{{ Z} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}}} + {{{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{{ K} _k} _l} _{,m}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _l} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _m} _p}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _l} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _m} _k} _p}}}} + {{{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _l} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _p} _k} _m}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _l} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _p} _m}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _l} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _m} _p} _k}}}} + {{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _l} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _p} _k} _m}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _k} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _m} _p}}}} + {{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _k} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _p} _l} _m}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _k} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _p} _m}}}} + {{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _k} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _p} _l} _m}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{{{{ K} _m} _n} _{,k}}}}} + {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _m} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _p}}} + {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _m} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _p}}} + {{{{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ Z} _m}} {{{{ K} _k} _l}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}}}} - {{{8}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\pi}} \cdot {{{ S} _k}}}} - {{{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}}}}}$

Bona-Masso shift evolution:
${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,t}} = {{ B} ^i}$

hyperbolic shift $B^i$ evolution:
${{{ B} ^i} _{,t}} = {{{{\frac{3}{4}}} {{{{ \bar{\Lambda}} ^i} _{,t}}}} - {{{\eta}} \cdot {{{ B} ^i}}}}$
